Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Comanche 44, the initial release (though not the final mission release) of the Apollo 10 Command Module (CM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) software. Subsequent releases were Comanche 45 and Comanche 45/2 (the flown release on Apollo 10). The reconstruction is believed to be exactly accurate, but in the absence of an actual Apollo-era listing of Comanche 44, some explanation of the reconstruction process is needed to insure confidence in that accuracy.

The starting point was the source code of Comanche 51 (separately previously reconstructed from an Apollo-era listing of Comanche 55, flown on Apollo 11). Comanche 51 source code was then modified by undoing changes known to have been made between revisions 44 and 51. The now-reconstructed Comanche 44 source code was verified by assembling it and checking that the assembled code had the expected known-correct memory-bank checksums. Note that page numbers in the reconstructed code match those on the Comanche 55 printout, although the source code would likely have different page numbers in a contemporary Comanche 44 listing.

Annotations that were not present in the contemporary source code have been added to the reconstructed code to justify each change relative to Comanche 51. Here's a guide to the Apollo documentation referenced in those annotations:
  • MIT/IL engineering drawing 2021153D, sheet 3. Listing of the memory-bank checksums for Comanche 44.
  • Comanche 55 (Apollo 11 CM) assembly listing.
  • Colossus 249 (Apollo 9 CM) assembly listing.
  • Guidance System Operations Plan for Colossus 3, Section 5, p. xiii. Table listing some Program Request Changes (PCRs) incorporated between Comanche 45/2 and Comanche 55.
  • Guidance System Operations Plan for Colossus 2E, Section 3, pp. ix-x. Tables listing some Program Change Requests (PCRs) incorporated between Comanche 44 and Comanche 55.
  • Programmed Guidance Equations for Colossus 2, Based on Comanche 55. A pseudocode representation of Comanche 55, showing change bars for differences from Comanche 45/2.
In most cases, only the titles (rather than the full texts) of PCRs are known. In addition to the explanatory annotations, there is also a step-by-step commentary about the reconstruction process.

Comments expected to have been present in the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC Project's GitHub repository. 

013038,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
013039,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    PINBALL_GAME__BUTTONS_AND_LIGHTS.agc
013040,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Comanche revision 044.
013041,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the
013042,000006:                                                                                                  ##              original release of the flight software for the Command
013043,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Module's (CM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 10.
013044,000008:                                                                                                  ##              The code has been recreated from a copy of Comanche 055. It
013045,000009:                                                                                                  ##              has been adapted such that the resulting bugger words
013046,000010:                                                                                                  ##              exactly match those specified for Comanche 44 in NASA drawing
013047,000011:                                                                                                  ##              2021153D, which gives relatively high confidence that the
013048,000012:                                                                                                  ##              reconstruction is correct.
013049,000013:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
013050,000014:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.

013058,000022:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
013059,000023:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4            DATE - 27 APRIL 1967            ASSEMBLY - PINDISK REV 17
013060,000024:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
013061,000025:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
013062,000026: 
013063,000027:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
013064,000028: 
013065,000029:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
013066,000030:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
013067,000031:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
013068,000032:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
013069,000033: 
013070,000034:                                                                                                  #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
013071,000035:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
013072,000036:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
013073,000037:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
013074,000038:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
013075,000039: 
013076,000040:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
013077,000041:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
013078,000042:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
013079,000043:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
013080,000044: 
013081,000045:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
013082,000046:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
013083,000047: 
013084,000048:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES-
013085,000049: 
013086,000050:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
013087,000051:                                                                                                  #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A MAIN (NAVIGATION) KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES
013088,000052:                                                                                                  #  INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1 (KEYRUPT2) AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO 
013089,000053:                                                                                                  #  CHANNEL 15 (CHANNEL 16).  KEYRUPT1 (KEYRUPT2) PLACES THE KEY
013090,000054:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
013091,000055:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
013092,000056: 
013093,000057:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
013094,000058:                                                                                                  #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
013095,000059:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
013096,000060:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
013097,000061: 
013098,000062:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
013099,000063:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
013100,000064:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
013101,000065:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
013102,000066:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
013103,000067: 
013104,000068:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
013105,000069: 
013106,000070:                                                                                                  #        IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
013107,000071:                                                                                                  #                1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.

Page 308 

013109,000073:                                                                                                  #                2)      EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE
013110,000074:                                                                                                  #                        PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
013111,000075:                                                                                                  #                        RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
013112,000076:                                                                                                  #                        CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
013113,000077:                                                                                                  #                        ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
013114,000078:                                                                                                  #                3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
013115,000079:                                                                                                  #                        SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
013116,000080:                                                                                                  #                        30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
013117,000081:                                                                                                  #                4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
013118,000082:                                                                                                  #                        ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
013119,000083:                                                                                                  #                        THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
013120,000084: 
013121,000085:                                                                                                  #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
013122,000086:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
013123,000087:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
013124,000088: 
013125,000089:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
013126,000090: 
013127,000091:                                                                                                  #        EXTERNAL INITIATION:
013128,000092:                                                                                                  #                IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
013129,000093:                                                                                                  #                ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
013130,000094: 
013131,000095:                                                                                                  #        INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
013132,000096:                                                                                                  #                IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
013133,000097:                                                                                                  #                (WITH OCTAL 01501).
013134,000098:                                                                                                  #                IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
013135,000099:                                                                                                  #                CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206).  THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
013136,000100:                                                                                                  #                1)      ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
013137,000101:                                                                                                  #                2)      NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
013138,000102: 
013139,000103:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
013140,000104:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
013141,000105: 
013142,000106:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT-
013143,000107: 
013144,000108:                                                                                                  #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
013145,000109:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
013146,000110:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
013147,000111:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
013148,000112: 
013149,000113:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION-
013150,000114: 
013151,000115:                                                                                                  #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
013152,000116:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
013153,000117:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
013154,000118:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
013155,000119:

Page 309 

013157,000121:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR
013158,000122:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
013159,000123: 
013160,000124:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST-
013161,000125: 
013162,000126:                                                                                                  #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
013163,000127:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
013164,000128: 
013165,000129:                                                                                                  #        NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
013166,000130:                                                                                                  #                        OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
013167,000131:                                                                                                  #                                                NVSUBUSY
013168,000132:                                                                                                  #                                                PRENVBSY
013169,000133: 
013170,000134:                                                                                                  #        ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
013171,000135:                                                                                                  #                        AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
013172,000136: 
013173,000137:                                                                                                  #        DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
013174,000138:                                                                                                  #                        PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
013175,000139:                                                                                                  #                        (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
013176,000140:                                                                                                  #                        FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
013177,000141: 
013178,000142:                                                                                                  #        BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
013179,000143:                                                                                                  #                        COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
013180,000144: 
013181,000145:                                                                                                  #        JAMTERM         ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
013182,000146:                                                                                                  #        JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V33) FUNCTION.
013183,000147: 
013184,000148:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
013185,000149: 
013186,000150:                                                                                                  #        PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
013187,000151:                                                                                                  #                REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
013188,000152:                                                                                                  #                THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
013189,000153:                                                                                                  #                SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
013190,000154: 
013191,000155:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
013192,000156:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
013193,000157: 
013194,000158:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
013195,000159:                                                                                                  #        TABLES:.
013196,000160: 
013197,000161:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
013198,000162:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
013199,000163:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.

(Note that this doc by Green and Filene is/was available online at http://hrst.mit.edu/hrs/apollo/public/archive/1706.pdf — RSB 6/2004.)

013215,000179:                                                                                                  # DSPCOUNT       ERASE                   DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
013216,000180:                                                                                                  # DECBRNCH       ERASE                   +DEC, -DEC, OCT INDICATOR
013217,000181:                                                                                                  # VERBREG        ERASE                   VERB CODE
013218,000182:                                                                                                  # NOUNREG        ERASE                   NOUN CODE
013219,000183:                                                                                                  # XREG           ERASE                   R1 INPUT BUFFER
013220,000184:                                                                                                  # YREG           ERASE                   R2 INPUT BUFFER
013221,000185:                                                                                                  # ZREG           ERASE                   R3 INPUT BUFFER
013222,000186:                                                                                                  # XREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013223,000187:                                                                                                  # YREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013224,000188:                                                                                                  # HITEMOUT       =       YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
013225,000189:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
013226,000190:                                                                                                  # ZREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013227,000191:                                                                                                  # LOTEMOUT       =       ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
013228,000192:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
013229,000193:                                                                                                  # MODREG         ERASE                   MODE CODE
013230,000194:                                                                                                  # DSPLOCK        ERASE                   KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
013231,000195:                                                                                                  # REQRET         ERASE                   RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
013232,000196:                                                                                                  # LOADSTAT       ERASE                   STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
013233,000197:                                                                                                  # CLPASS         ERASE                   PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
013234,000198:                                                                                                  # NOUT           ERASE                   ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
013235,000199:                                                                                                  # NOUNCADR       ERASE                   MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
013236,000200:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE        ERASE                   N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
013237,000201:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE1       ERASE                   NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR(MATBS) = MONSAVE+1
013238,000202:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE2       ERASE                   NVMONOPT OPTIONS
013239,000203:                                                                                                  # DSPTAB         ERASE   +13D            0-10, DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER. 11-13, C RELAYS
013240,000204:                                                                                                  # CADRSTOR       ERASE                   ENDIDLE STORAGE
013241,000205:                                                                                                  # NVQTEM         ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
013242,000206:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
013243,000207:                                                                                                  # NVBNKTEM       ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
013244,000208:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVQTEM+1
013245,000209:                                                                                                  # VERBSAVE       ERASE                   NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
013246,000210:                                                                                                  # DSPLIST        ERASE                   WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
013247,000211:                                                                                                  # EXTVBACT       REASE                   EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
013248,000212:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM1        ERASE   +2              BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
013249,000213:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM2        ERASE   +2              BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
013250,000214:

013308,000272:                                                                                                  # IDAD2TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
013309,000273:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+1, = IDAD3TEM-1.
013310,000274:                                                                                                  # IDAD3TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
013311,000275:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+2, = IDAD2TEM+1.
013312,000276:                                                                                                  # RUTMXTEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR SF ROUT TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN ONLY)
013313,000277: 
013314,000278:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013315,000279: 
013316,000280:                                                                                                  #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013317,000281: 
013318,000282:                                                                                                  #        MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
013319,000283:                                                                                                  #        BUF, +1, +2
013320,000284:                                                                                                  #        BUF2, +1, +2
013321,000285:                                                                                                  #        MPTEMP
013322,000286:                                                                                                  #        ADDRWD
013323,000287: 
013324,000288:                                                                                                  #  END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION
013325,000289: 
013326,000290:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013327,000291: 
013328,000292:                                                                                                  # DSPCNT         ERASE                   COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
013329,000293:                                                                                                  # UPLOCK         ERASE                   BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
013330,000294:                                                                                                  #                                        RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
013331,000295: 
013332,000296:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013333,000297: 
013334,000298:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013335,000299: 
013336,000300:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP1       =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
013337,000301:                                                                                                  # DSRUPTEM       =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR DSPOUT
013338,000302:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP2       =       RUPTAGN         TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
013339,000303: 
013340,000304:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013341,000305:

Page 313 

013343,000307:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
013344,000308:                                                                                                  #        0               10000
013345,000309:                                                                                                  #        1               00001
013346,000310:                                                                                                  #        9               01001
013347,000311:                                                                                                  #        VERB            10001
013348,000312:                                                                                                  #        ERROR RES       10010
013349,000313:                                                                                                  #        KEY RLSE        11001
013350,000314:                                                                                                  #        +               11010
013351,000315:                                                                                                  #        -               11011
013352,000316:                                                                                                  #        ENTER           11100
013353,000317:                                                                                                  #        CLEAR           11110
013354,000318:                                                                                                  #        NOUN            11111
013355,000319: 
013356,000320:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
013357,000321:                                                                                                  #  A-S   SELECT A RELAYWORD.  THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
013358,000322:                                                                                                  #        ENERGIZED.
013359,000323:                                                                                                  #  B     FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
013360,000324:                                                                                                  #  C-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
013361,000325:                                                                                                  #  D-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
013362,000326: 
013363,000327:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
013364,000328:                                                                                                  #        MD1             MD2 (MAJOR MODE)
013365,000329:                                                                                                  #        VD1             VD2 (VERB)                      ND1             ND2 (NOUN)
013366,000330:                                                                                                  #        R1D1            R1D2            R1D3            R1D4            R1D5 (R1)
013367,000331:                                                                                                  #        R2D1            R2D2            R2D3            R2D4            R2D5 (R2)
013368,000332:                                                                                                  #        R3D1            R3D2            R3D3            R3D4            R3D5 (R3)
013369,000333: 
013370,000334:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
013371,000335: 
013372,000336:                                                                                                  #        MD1     25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
013373,000337:                                                                                                  #        MD2     24              R2D2    10
013374,000338:                                                                                                  #        VD1     23              R2D3    7
013375,000339:                                                                                                  #        VD2     22              R2D4    6
013376,000340:                                                                                                  #        ND1     21              R2D5    5
013377,000341:                                                                                                  #        ND2     20              R3D1    4
013378,000342:                                                                                                  #        R1D1    16              R3D2    3
013379,000343:                                                                                                  #        R1D2    15              R3D3    2
013380,000344:                                                                                                  #        R1D3    14              R3D4    1
013381,000345:                                                                                                  #        R1D4    13              R3D5    0
013382,000346:                                                                                                  #        R1D5    12
013383,000347: 
013384,000348:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
013385,000349: 
013386,000350:                                                                                                  #        DSPTAB          RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
013387,000351:                                                                                                  #        RELADD
013388,000352:                                                                                                  #        10              1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2  (24)
013389,000353:                                                                                                  #        9               1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2  (22)
013390,000354:                                                                                                  #        8               1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2  (20)
013391,000355:                                                                                                  #        7               1000                                            R1D1 (16)

Page 314 

013393,000357:                                                                                                  #        6               0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
013394,000358:                                                                                                  #        5               0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
013395,000359:                                                                                                  #        4               0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
013396,000360:                                                                                                  #        3               0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
013397,000361:                                                                                                  #        2               0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
013398,000362:                                                                                                  #        1               0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
013399,000363:                                                                                                  #        0               0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
013400,000364:                                                                                                  #                        0000        NO RELAYWORD
013401,000365: 
013402,000366:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
013403,000367: 
013404,000368:                                                                                                  #        BLANK   00000
013405,000369:                                                                                                  #        0       10101
013406,000370:                                                                                                  #        1       00011
013407,000371:                                                                                                  #        2       11001
013408,000372:                                                                                                  #        3       11011
013409,000373:                                                                                                  #        4       01111
013410,000374:                                                                                                  #        5       11110
013411,000375:                                                                                                  #        6       11100
013412,000376:                                                                                                  #        7       10011
013413,000377:                                                                                                  #        8       11101
013414,000378:                                                                                                  #        9       11111
013415,000379: 
013416,000380:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
013417,000381: 
013418,000382:                                                                                                  #        KEY RELEASE LIGHT       -       BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
013419,000383:                                                                                                  #        VERB/NOUN FLASH         -       BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
013420,000384:                                                                                                  #        OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT    -       BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11

014110,001074:

Page 330 

014112,001076:                                                                                                  #  NOUN TABLES
014113,001077: 
014114,001078:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
014115,001079:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE ECADR FOR EACH NOUN.
014116,001080:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.  - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR (E OR F) TO
014117,001081:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED.  -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
014118,001082:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
014119,001083: 
014120,001084:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
014121,001085:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
014122,001086: 
014123,001087:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
014124,001088: 
014125,001089:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,  M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
014126,001090:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
014127,001091:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
014128,001092: 
014129,001093:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,           M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
014130,001094:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
014131,001095:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
014132,001096:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
014133,001097:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
014134,001098:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
014135,001099: 
014136,001100:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
014137,001101:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.  IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
014138,001102:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
014139,001103: 
014140,001104:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
014141,001105:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
014142,001106: 
014143,001107:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
014144,001108:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
014145,001109: 
014146,001110:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
014147,001111: 
014148,001112:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER          3 COMPONENT CASE
014149,001113:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
014150,001114:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
014151,001115:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER          2 COMPONENT CASE
014152,001116:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
014153,001117: 
014154,001118:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
014155,001119:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
014156,001120:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
014157,001121: 
014158,001122:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
014159,001123:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED.  ALARM IF VIOLATION.
014160,001124: 
014161,001125:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
014162,001126:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER.  IF NOT, ALARM.
014163,001127:

Page 331 

014165,001129:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY VERBS
014166,001130: 
014167,001131: 41,2353           45016        DSPABC             CS       TWO                                   
014168,001132: 41,2354           02424                           TC       COMPTEST

014684,001648:                                                                                                  #  WORD AS 10 DECIMAL DIGITS ON THE AGC DISPLAY PANEL.  IT CAN BE USED WITH
014685,001649:                                                                                                  #  ANY NOUN, EXCEPT MIXED NOUNS.  IT DISPLAYS THE CONTENTS
014686,001650:                                                                                                  #  OF THE REGISTER NOUNADD IS POINTING TO.  IF USED WITH NOUNS WHICH ARE
014687,001651:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.

Page 355 

015293,002257:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY.  IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
015294,002258:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
015295,002259:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
015296,002260:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
015297,002261:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
015298,002262: 
015299,002263:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
015300,002264:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET.  IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
015301,002265:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE.  IT SAVES
015302,002266:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  BIT 15 OF
015303,002267:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT).  BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
015304,002268:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
015305,002269:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT).  IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
015306,002270: 
015307,002271:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
015308,002272:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
015309,002273:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
015310,002274: 
015311,002275:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
015312,002276:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
015313,002277: 
015314,002278:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
015315,002279:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
015316,002280: 
015317,002281:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW

015446,002410: 
015447,002411:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
015448,002412:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  THE FCADR OF THE 
015449,002413:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN.  IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
015450,002414:                                                                                                  #  
015451,002415:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
015452,002416: 
015453,002417:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
015454,002418:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
015455,002419:                                                                                                  #        V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
015456,002420: 
015457,002421:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
015458,002422:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                             V27N01E(FCADR)E
015459,002423:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,     V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E     V27N01E(FCADR)E
015460,002424:

015462,002426: 41,3354           54777                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
015463,002427: 41,3355           31047                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
015464,002428: 41,3356           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
015465,002429: 41,3357           31017                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
015466,002430: 41,3360           04715                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.

015882,002846:                                                                                                  #  (MAIN USE IS INTENDED AS RESPONSE TO INTERNALLY INITIATED FLASHING
015883,002847:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAYS IN ENDIDLE.  SHOULD NOT BE USED WITH LOAD VERBS, PLEASE PERFORM,
015884,002848:                                                                                                  #  OR PLEASE MARK VERBS BECAUSE THEY ALREADY USE L+3 IN ANOTHER CONTEXT.)
015885,002849: 
015886,002850: 40,3364           45021        VBRESEQ            CS       ZERO                                  #  MAKE IT LOOK LIKE DATA IN.
015887,002851: 40,3365           03350                           TC       VBPROC     +1                         
015888,002852: 
015889,002853:                                                                                                  #  FLASH IS TURNED OFF BY PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE,
015890,002854:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.

Page 368 

015892,002856: 
015893,002857:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
015894,002858: 
015895,002859:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
015896,002860: 
015897,002861:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
015898,002862:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
015899,002863:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
015900,002864:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
015901,002865: 
015902,002866:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
015903,002867:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
015904,002868:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
015905,002869: 
015906,002870:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
015907,002871:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
015908,002872:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
015909,002873:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
015910,002874:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
015911,002875:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
015912,002876:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES.  HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
015913,002877:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
015914,002878:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
015915,002879:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
015916,002880:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
015917,002881: 
015918,002882: 40,3366           45015        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
015919,002883: 40,3367           00006                           EXTEND                                         
015920,002884: 40,3370           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
015921,002885: 40,3371           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
015922,002886: 40,3372           35002                           CAF      BIT14                                 
015923,002887: 40,3373           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
015924,002888: 40,3374           10000                           CCS      A                                     
015925,002889: 40,3375           03404                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
015926,002890: 40,3376           04473        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
015927,002891: 40,3377           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
015928,002892: 40,3400           03402                           TC       +2                                    #        DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
015929,002893: 40,3401           05217                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
015930,002894: 40,3402           04701                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
015931,002895: 40,3403           21272                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
015932,002896: 40,3404           35021        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
015933,002897: 40,3405           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #        JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
015934,002898: 40,3406           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
015935,002899: 40,3407           05217                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #        CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
015936,002900: 40,3410           04516                           TC       RELDSP1                               
015937,002901: 40,3411           05217                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
015938,002902: 
015939,002903: 40,3412                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
015940,002904:

Page 369 

015942,002906:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER.  IT CAN BE
015943,002907:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
015944,002908:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
015945,002909:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
015946,002910:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
015947,002911: 
015948,002912:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
015949,002913:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
015950,002914:                                                                                                  #  -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
015951,002915: 
015952,002916:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
015953,002917:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
015954,002918: 
015955,002919:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
015956,002920:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE.  THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
015957,002921:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
015958,002922:                                                                                                  #  ACTION).  IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
015959,002923:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
015960,002924: 
015961,002925:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
015962,002926:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
015963,002927:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
015964,002928:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
015965,002929: 
015966,002930:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
015967,002931:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
015968,002932:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
015969,002933:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
015970,002934:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
015971,002935:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
015972,002936:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
015973,002937: 
015974,002938:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
015975,002939:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
015976,002940: 
015977,002941:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
015978,002942:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
015979,002943: 
015980,002944:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
015981,002945:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
015982,002946: 
015983,002947:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
015984,002948:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
015985,002949:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THEREGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
015986,002950:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
015987,002951:                                                                                                  #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
015988,002952:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS.  THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
015989,002953:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
015990,002954: 
015991,002955:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 370 

015993,002957:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L.  IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
015994,002958:                                                                                                  #  A.  AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
015995,002959:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
015996,002960:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L.  IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
015997,002961:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS.  (THIS VERB
015998,002962:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
015999,002963:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
016000,002964:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
016001,002965:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
016002,002966: 
016003,002967:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
016004,002968:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET.  (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
016005,002969: 
016006,002970:    4170                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
016007,002971: 
016008,002972:    4170                                           COUNT    02/PIN                                
016009,002973:
