016114,003078:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN ENTPAS0 (INTMCTBS).
016115,003079: 
016116,003080:    4220                                           SETLOC   NVSUBEND   +2                         
016117,003081:    4220                                           COUNT    02/PIN                                
016118,003082:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
016119,003083:    4220           35001        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #        THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
016120,003084:    4221           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
016121,003085:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR BIT.
016122,003086:    4222           00002                           TC       Q                                     
016123,003087: 
016124,003088:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA).  SET BY NVSUB
016125,003089:                                                                                                  #                +1      PROCEED NO DATA.  SET BY SPECIAL VERB
016126,003090:                                                                                                  #                -1      TERMINATE       SET BY SPECIAL VERB
016127,003091:                                                                                                  #                -0      DATA IN         SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
016128,003092:                                                                                                  #                        OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
016129,003093: 
016130,003094:                                                                                                  #  L TC ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED)
016131,003095:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
016132,003096:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED.  ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
016133,003097:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
016134,003098:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
016135,003099:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
016136,003100:                                                                                                  #        L+1     FOR TERMINATE
016137,003101:                                                                                                  #        L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
016138,003102:                                                                                                  #        L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
016139,003103:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.

Page 373 

016141,003105: 
016142,003106:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP
016143,003107:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
016144,003108:                                                                                                  #        1)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
016145,003109:                                                                                                  #                EXCEEDED.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
016146,003110:                                                                                                  #        2)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
016147,003111:                                                                                                  #                NVSUBUSY.
016148,003112: 
016149,003113:    4223           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
016150,003114:    4224           04234                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
016151,003115:    4225           04240                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
016152,003116:    4226           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
016153,003117:    4227           75054                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
016154,003118:    4230           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
016155,003119:    4231           55042                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
016156,003120:    4232           05175                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
016157,003121: 
016158,003122:    4233           05217        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
016159,003123: 
016160,003124:    4234           11042        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
016161,003125:    4235           04243                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.
016162,003126:    4236           00002                           TC       Q

Page 381 

016491,003455:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016492,003456: 
016493,003457:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
016494,003458:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR.  THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
016495,003459:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
016496,003460:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
016497,003461: 
016498,003462:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
016499,003463:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1)      BY ENDIDLE
016500,003464:                                                                                                  #                2)      BY NVSUBUSY
016501,003465:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
016502,003466:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME.  IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
016503,003467:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY AJOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
016504,003468:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
016505,003469: 
016506,003470:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
016507,003471:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
016508,003472:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
016509,003473:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
016510,003474:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
016511,003475: 
016512,003476:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
016513,003477:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
016514,003478:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM.  NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
016515,003479:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
016516,003480:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
016517,003481: 
016518,003482:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
016519,003483:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
016520,003484:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
016521,003485:                                                                                                  #  .
016522,003486: 
016523,003487:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
016524,003488:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION).  IT IS
016525,003489:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
016526,003490:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
016527,003491: 
016528,003492:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
016529,003493:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
016530,003494:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
016531,003495: 
016532,003496:                                                                                                  #        1)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
016533,003497:                                                                                                  #                IS EXCEEDED.
016534,003498:                                                                                                  #        2)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 382 

016536,003500:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
016537,003501: 
016538,003502:    4453           44460        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
016539,003503:    4454           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
016540,003504:    4455           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
016541,003505:    4456           04701        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
016542,003506:    4457           10577                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
016543,003507:    4460           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
016544,003508: 
016545,003509:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
016546,003510:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
016547,003511: 
016548,003512: 04,2577                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
016549,003513: 04,2577                                           COUNT    07/PIN                                
016550,003514: 
016551,003515: 04,2577           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
016552,003516: 04,2600           04234                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
016553,003517: 04,2601           04240                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
016554,003518: 04,2602           04410                           TC       RELDSPON                              
016555,003519: 04,2603           30001                           CA       L                                     
016556,003520: 04,2604           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
016557,003521: 04,2605           05175        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
016558,003522: 
016559,003523:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
016560,003524:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
016561,003525:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE).  IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
016562,003526:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
016563,003527:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
016564,003528: 
016565,003529:    4461                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
016566,003530:    4461                                           COUNT    02/PIN                                
016567,003531: 
016568,003532:    4461           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016569,003533:    4462           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
016570,003534:    4463           35002                           CAF      BIT14                                 
016571,003535:    4464           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
016572,003536:    4465           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
016573,003537:    4466           10000                           CCS      A                                     
016574,003538:    4467           14471                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
016575,003539:    4470           14200                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
016576,003540:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
016577,003541:    4471           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2.  PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
016578,003542:    4472           14453                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
016579,003543: 
016580,003544:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
016581,003545:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
016582,003546: 
016583,003547:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
016584,003548: 
016585,003549:    4473           56002        RELDSP             XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT

Page 383 

016587,003551:    4474           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  OFF, SEARCH DSPLIST
016588,003552:    4475           45002                           CS       BIT14                                 
016589,003553:    4476           00004                           INHINT                                         
016590,003554:    4477           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              
016591,003555:    4500           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
016592,003556:    4501           11043                           CCS      DSPLIST                               
016593,003557:    4502           04504                           TC       +2                                    
016594,003558:    4503           04507                           TC       RELDSP2                               #  LIST EMPTY
016595,003559:    4504           35021                           CAF      ZERO                                  
016596,003560:    4505           57043                           XCH      DSPLIST                               
016597,003561:    4506           05201                           TC       JOBWAKE                               
016598,003562:    4507           00003        RELDSP2            RELINT                                         
016599,003563:    4510           45013                           CS       BIT5                                  #  TURN OFF KEY RELEASE LIGHT

Reconstruction: In Comanche 51, the single line following this annotation is replaced by
   VBTSTLTS        TC      BANKCALL
                   CADR    CHKPOOH
                   INHINT
Thus, in Comanche 44, a call to CHKPOOH has been removed. This removal relates to Programmed Guidance Equations for Colossus 2, p. VBDF-2, though as usual in these situations, we simply fall back on Colossus 249 (Apollo 9) code rather than attempt to relate the pseudocode of the Programmed Guidance Equations to the actual assembly code.
